container that has already been passed to createRoot() before" typically happens when <code>createRoot()</code> is called more than once on the same DOM element.</p>
<p>Looking at the App.tsx file, I see:</p>
<pre><code>createRoot(document.getElementById("root")!).render(&lt;App /&gt;);
</code></pre>
<p>This is being called once at the module level, which should be fine. However, the warning suggests that <code>createRoot()</code> is being called multiple times on the same element.</p>
<p>This could happen if:</p>
<ol>
<li>The App.tsx file is being imported/executed multiple times</li>
<li>There's a Hot Module Replacement (HMR) issue where the module is being re-executed</li>
<li>There's a duplicate root creation somewhere in the code</li>
</ol>
<p>The most common cause in a Vite + React setup with HMR is that the module gets re-executed when hot modules reload, and createRoot gets called again on the same element.</p>
<p>The fix is to check if a root already exists before creating a new one, or to store the root reference and reuse it.</p>
<p>Let me check the App.tsx to see how it's structured and fix it properly.</p>

When HMR happens, the module gets re-executed and createRoot gets called again on the same element. The fix is to either:</p>
<ol>
<li>Check if the root element already has a root attached</li>
<li>Store the root reference and reuse it</li>
<li>Only call createRoot once and never re-execute that code</li>
</ol>
<p>The best approach is to check if a root already exists before creating a new one. However, there's no public API to check if an element already has a root. The standard approach is to store the root in a variable at module scope and check if it exists.</p>
<p>Actually, a simpler approach that's more idiomatic for modern React is to only call createRoot and render once, and not re-execute on HMR. We can do this by wrapping the createRoot call in a way that prevents re-execution.</p>
<p>Let me use the standard pattern of storing the root and checking if it exists:</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-spinnerMessage" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="spinner-message block-node css-1h2sv0j" data-status="stop"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="tabler-icon tabler-icon-check css-13z620h"><title>09:15:50 PM</title><path d="M5 12l5 5l10 -10"></path></svg><div class="css-1rr4qq7"><span class="jss3719 jss3727 css-1i415sy">Thinking</span><div class="css-9z0acm"><div class="css-1e8hpf3"><div><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p>Actually, <code>_reactRootContainer</code> is an internal property and might not be reliable. A better approach is to use the standard pattern from React 18 docs. Let me use a more robust approach with a try-catch or by storing the root in a module-level variable that won't get re-executed.</p>
<p>Actually, the simplest and most robust solution is to check if the element already has React content. But since we don't have direct access to check, the safest approach is to wrap the root creation in a way that only executes once.</p>
<p>Let me try a different approach - using a module-level variable to store the root:</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-spinnerMessage" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="spinner-message block-node css-1h2sv0j" data-status="stop"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="tabler-icon tabler-icon-check css-13z620h"><title>09:15:50 PM</title><path d="M5 12l5 5l10 -10"></path></svg><div class="css-1rr4qq7"><span class="jss3719 jss3727 css-1i415sy">Thinking</span><div class="css-9z0acm"><div class="css-1e8hpf3"><div><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p>Actually, I realize the real issue. When HMR reloads the module, it re-executes the entire module including the createRoot call. The warning happens because createRoot is being called twice on the same element.</p>
<p>The best solution for HMR is actually to use the conditional check properly. However, looking at Vite's React template, they actually don't guard the createRoot call - they rely on React to handle it gracefully.</p>
<p>Let me check if there's a different issue. The error message suggests createRoot is being called twice. This could also happen if:</p>
<ol>
<li>There's duplicate imports or App.tsx being imported twice</li>
<li>There's an issue with how the dev server is set up</li>
<li>There's actual duplicate root creation code somewhere</li>

<p>Actually, the simplest fix that works well with Vite's HMR is to just let React handle it. But the warning persists. Let me use a more defensive approach with a module-level guard:</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-markdownText" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="markdown-text block-node"><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p> Actually, the issue is that the module gets re-executed on HMR. Let me use a module-level guard that only allows root creation once:</p>
</div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-spinnerMessage" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="spinner-message block-node css-1h2sv0j" data-status="stop"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="tabler-icon tabler-icon-check css-13z620h"><title>09:15:50 PM</title><path d="M5 12l5 5l10 -10"></path></svg><div class="css-1rr4qq7"><span class="jss3719 jss3727 css-1i415sy">Thinking</span><div class="css-9z0acm"><div class="css-1e8hpf3"><div><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p>This solution uses a window flag to ensure createRoot is only called once, even if the module gets re-executed during HMR. This is a common pattern for handling HMR in Vite + React projects.</p>
<p>However, there's a downside - with this approach, HMR won't properly update the App component on changes since we're not re-rendering. For a better HMR experience, we should store the root and call root.render() on updates.</p>
<p>Let me implement the proper HMR-aware pattern:</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-markdownText" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="markdown-text block-node"><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p> Let me improve this to properly support HMR updates:</p>
</div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-spinnerMessage" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="spinner-message block-node css-1h2sv0j" data-status="stop"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="tabler-icon tabler-icon-check css-13z620h"><title>09:15:50 PM</title><path d="M5 12l5 5l10 -10"></path></svg><div class="css-1rr4qq7"><span class="jss3719 jss3727 css-1i415sy">Thinking</span><div class="css-9z0acm"><div class="css-1e8hpf3"><div><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p>Perfect! Now I've created a solution that:</p>
<ol>
<li>Stores the root in a window variable on first render</li>
<li>Reuses that root on subsequent renders (HMR updates)</li>
<li>Only calls createRoot() once</li>
<li>Calls root.render() each time with the updated App component</li>
</ol>
<p>This should eliminate the warning about calling createRoot() multiple times while still supporting HMR properly.</p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-renderer node-markdownText" contenteditable="false"><div data-node-view-wrapper="" style="white-space: normal;"><div class="markdown-text block-node"><div class="css-1gn5aju"><p> ‚úÖ <strong>Fixed!</strong> The issue was that <code>createRoot()</code> was being called multiple times on the same DOM element during Hot Module Replacement (HMR).</p>
<p><strong>The solution:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Store the React root in a window variable on first creation</li>
<li>On HMR updates, reuse the existing root and just call <code>render()</code> with the updated component</li>
<li>This prevents the "createRoot called twice" warning while maintaining proper HMR support</li>
</ul>
<p>The warning should now be gone. The app will still update properly when you make changes to the code!</p>

const renderApp = () =&gt; {
  const container = document.getElementById("root");
  if (!container) return;

  if (!(window as any).__app_root__) {
    (window as any).__app_root__ = createRoot(container);
  }

  (window as any).__app_root__.render(&lt;App /&gt;);
};

renderApp();
</code></pre>

The fix is already in place. The code at the bottom of <code>client/App.tsx</code> includes:</p>
<pre><code>// Create root once and reuse on HMR updates
const renderApp = () =&gt; {
  const container = document.getElementById("root");
  if (!container) return;

  if (!(window as any).__app_root__) {
    (window as any).__app_root__ = createRoot(container);
  }

  (window as any).__app_root__.render(&lt;App /&gt;);
};

renderApp();
</code></pre>
<p>This fix ensures that <code>createRoot()</code> is only called once by storing the root instance on the <code>window</code> object. On subsequent renders (like during HMR), it reuses the existing root and just calls <code>.render()</code> on it.</p>

1.  **Primary Request and Intent:**
    The user's overarching goal is to develop the MyHealthAlly application with a clear separation of concerns: patient-facing interfaces will be managed by Builder CMS, and clinician-facing interfaces will be built using React. The user has provided detailed specifications for 24 patient-facing screens and expects them to be fully completed in Builder CMS. <li><strong>Changes Made:</strong> The <code>createRoot()</code> logic was updated to prevent the "called twice" warning during HMR by implementing a module-level guard and reusing the root element.</li>
<li><strong>Important Code Snippet (Recent Fix):</strong><pre><code>// Create root once and reuse on HMR updates
const renderApp = () =&gt; {
  const container = document.getElementById("root");
  if (!container) return;

  if (!(window as any).__app_root__) {
    (window as any).__app_root__ = createRoot(container);
  }

  (window as any).__app_root__.render(&lt;App /&gt;);
};

renderApp();
</code></pre>
</li>
